Location: Excellent location, located in the southwest corner of Baotu Spring Park. The hotel is built around Bailong Spring on three sides. You can enjoy the panoramic view of Bailong Spring from the room window. Outside the hotel is the Hui Muslim District of Jinan. I strongly recommend you to try the beef biscuits and beef soup. They are very good. In addition, the halal barbecue is also good.
Hardware: The room area is slightly small, but the facilities are very good. Our room is east-facing. There is a bay window in the room. You can sit and drink tea and look at Bailong Spring. It is very beautiful.
Software: After the first stay, I specially booked the room from the last time with the front desk before booking the second time. I am very grateful to the front desk staff. The front desk and room service staff are very polite and kind. They also gave free breakfast.
Breakfast: The variety is quite complete. It is not rich, but it is absolutely no problem to meet the requirements of eating well.
